7298             Class<?> ttype = body.type().parameterType(returnType == void.class ? 0 : 1);
7299             MethodType nextValType = nextRaw.type().changeReturnType(ttype);
7300 
7301             // perform the asType transforms under an exception transformer, as per spec.:
7302             try {
7303                 startIter = startIter.asType(iteratorType);
7304                 nextVal = nextRaw.asType(nextValType);
7305             } catch (WrongMethodTypeException ex) {
7306                 throw new IllegalArgumentException(ex);
7307             }
7308         }
7309 
7310         MethodHandle retv = null, step = body;
7311         if (returnType != void.class) {
7312             // the simple thing first:  in (I V A...), drop the I to get V
7313             retv = dropArguments(identity(returnType), 0, Iterator.class);
7314             // body type signature (V T A...), internal loop types (I V A...)
7315             step = swapArguments(body, 0, 1);  // swap V <-> T
7316         }
7317 
7318         MethodHandle[]
7319             iterVar    = { startIter, null, hasNext, retv },
7320             bodyClause = { init, filterArgument(step, 0, nextVal) };
7321         return loop(iterVar, bodyClause);
7322     }
7323 
7324     private static Class<?> iteratedLoopChecks(MethodHandle iterator, MethodHandle init, MethodHandle body) {
7325         Objects.requireNonNull(body);
7326         MethodType bodyType = body.type();
7327         Class<?> returnType = bodyType.returnType();
7328         List<Class<?>> internalParamList = bodyType.parameterList();
7329         // strip leading V value if present
7330         int vsize = (returnType == void.class ? 0 : 1);
7331         if (vsize != 0 && (internalParamList.size() == 0 || internalParamList.get(0) != returnType)) {
7332             // argument list has no "V" => error
7333             MethodType expected = bodyType.insertParameterTypes(0, returnType);
7334             throw misMatchedTypes("body function", bodyType, expected);
7335         } else if (internalParamList.size() <= vsize) {
7336             // missing T type => error
7337             MethodType expected = bodyType.insertParameterTypes(vsize, Object.class);
7338             throw misMatchedTypes("body function", bodyType, expected);
7339         }
7340         List<Class<?>> externalParamList = internalParamList.subList(vsize + 1, internalParamList.size());
7341         Class<?> iterableType = null;
7342         if (iterator != null) {
7343             // special case; if the body handle only declares V and T then
7344             // the external parameter list is obtained from iterator handle
7345             if (externalParamList.isEmpty()) {
7346                 externalParamList = iterator.type().parameterList();
7347             }
7348             MethodType itype = iterator.type();
7349             if (!Iterator.class.isAssignableFrom(itype.returnType())) {
7350                 throw newIllegalArgumentException("iteratedLoop first argument must have Iterator return type");
7351             }
7352             if (!itype.effectivelyIdenticalParameters(0, externalParamList)) {
7353                 MethodType expected = methodType(itype.returnType(), externalParamList);
7354                 throw misMatchedTypes("iterator parameters", itype, expected);
7355             }
7356         } else {
7357             if (externalParamList.isEmpty()) {
7358                 // special case; if the iterator handle is null and the body handle
7359                 // only declares V and T then the external parameter list consists
7360                 // of Iterable
7361                 externalParamList = Arrays.asList(Iterable.class);
7362                 iterableType = Iterable.class;
7363             } else {
7364                 // special case; if the iterator handle is null and the external
7365                 // parameter list is not empty then the first parameter must be
7366                 // assignable to Iterable
7367                 iterableType = externalParamList.get(0);
7368                 if (!Iterable.class.isAssignableFrom(iterableType)) {
7369                     throw newIllegalArgumentException(
7370                             "inferred first loop argument must inherit from Iterable: " + iterableType);
7371                 }
7372             }
7373         }
7374         if (init != null) {
7375             MethodType initType = init.type();
7376             if (initType.returnType() != returnType ||
7377                     !initType.effectivelyIdenticalParameters(0, externalParamList)) {
7378                 throw misMatchedTypes("loop initializer", initType, methodType(returnType, externalParamList));
7379             }
7380         }
7381         return iterableType;  // help the caller a bit
7382     }
7383 
7384     /*non-public*/
7385     static MethodHandle swapArguments(MethodHandle mh, int i, int j) {
7386         // there should be a better way to uncross my wires
7387         int arity = mh.type().parameterCount();
7388         int[] order = new int[arity];
7389         for (int k = 0; k < arity; k++)  order[k] = k;
7390         order[i] = j; order[j] = i;
7391         Class<?>[] types = mh.type().parameterArray();
7392         Class<?> ti = types[i]; types[i] = types[j]; types[j] = ti;
7393         MethodType swapType = methodType(mh.type().returnType(), types);
7394         return permuteArguments(mh, swapType, order);
7395     }
7396 
7397     /**
7398      * Makes a method handle that adapts a {@code target} method handle by wrapping it in a {@code try-finally} block.
7399      * Another method handle, {@code cleanup}, represents the functionality of the {@code finally} block. Any exception
7400      * thrown during the execution of the {@code target} handle will be passed to the {@code cleanup} handle. The
7401      * exception will be rethrown, unless {@code cleanup} handle throws an exception first.  The
7402      * value returned from the {@code cleanup} handle's execution will be the result of the execution of the
7403      * {@code try-finally} handle.
7404      * <p>
7405      * The {@code cleanup} handle will be passed one or two additional leading arguments.
7406      * The first is the exception thrown during the
7407      * execution of the {@code target} handle, or {@code null} if no exception was thrown.
7408      * The second is the result of the execution of the {@code target} handle, or, if it throws an exception,
7409      * a {@code null}, zero, or {@code false} value of the required type is supplied as a placeholder.
7410      * The second argument is not present if the {@code target} handle has a {@code void} return type.
7411      * (Note that, except for argument type conversions, combinators represent {@code void} values in parameter lists
7412      * by omitting the corresponding paradoxical arguments, not by inserting {@code null} or zero values.)
7413      * <p>
7414      * The {@code target} and {@code cleanup} handles must have the same corresponding argument and return types, except
7415      * that the {@code cleanup} handle may omit trailing arguments. Also, the {@code cleanup} handle must have one or
7416      * two extra leading parameters:<ul>
7417      * <li>a {@code Throwable}, which will carry the exception thrown by the {@code target} handle (if any); and
7418      * <li>a parameter of the same type as the return type of both {@code target} and {@code cleanup}, which will carry
7419      * the result from the execution of the {@code target} handle.
7420      * This parameter is not present if the {@code target} returns {@code void}.
7421      * </ul>
7422      * <p>
7423      * The pseudocode for the resulting adapter looks as follows. In the code, {@code V} represents the result type of
7424      * the {@code try/finally} construct; {@code A}/{@code a}, the types and values of arguments to the resulting
7425      * handle consumed by the cleanup; and {@code B}/{@code b}, those of arguments to the resulting handle discarded by
7426      * the cleanup.
7427      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
7428      * V target(A..., B...);
7429      * V cleanup(Throwable, V, A...);
7430      * V adapter(A... a, B... b) {
7431      *   V result = (zero value for V);
7432      *   Throwable throwable = null;
7433      *   try {
7434      *     result = target(a..., b...);
7435      *   } catch (Throwable t) {
7436      *     throwable = t;
7437      *     throw t;
7438      *   } finally {
7439      *     result = cleanup(throwable, result, a...);
7440      *   }
7441      *   return result;
7442      * }
7443      * }</pre></blockquote>
7444      * <p>
7445      * Note that the saved arguments ({@code a...} in the pseudocode) cannot
7446      * be modified by execution of the target, and so are passed unchanged
7447      * from the caller to the cleanup, if it is invoked.
7448      * <p>
7449      * The target and cleanup must return the same type, even if the cleanup
7450      * always throws.
7451      * To create such a throwing cleanup, compose the cleanup logic
7452      * with {@link #throwException throwException},
7453      * in order to create a method handle of the correct return type.
7454      * <p>
7455      * Note that {@code tryFinally} never converts exceptions into normal returns.
7456      * In rare cases where exceptions must be converted in that way, first wrap
7457      * the target with {@link #catchException(MethodHandle, Class, MethodHandle)}
7458      * to capture an outgoing exception, and then wrap with {@code tryFinally}.
7459      * <p>
7460      * It is recommended that the first parameter type of {@code cleanup} be
7461      * declared {@code Throwable} rather than a narrower subtype.  This ensures
7462      * {@code cleanup} will always be invoked with whatever exception that
7463      * {@code target} throws.  Declaring a narrower type may result in a
7464      * {@code ClassCastException} being thrown by the {@code try-finally}
7465      * handle if the type of the exception thrown by {@code target} is not
7466      * assignable to the first parameter type of {@code cleanup}.  Note that
7467      * various exception types of {@code VirtualMachineError},
7468      * {@code LinkageError}, and {@code RuntimeException} can in principle be
7469      * thrown by almost any kind of Java code, and a finally clause that
7470      * catches (say) only {@code IOException} would mask any of the others
7471      * behind a {@code ClassCastException}.
7472      *
7473      * @param target the handle whose execution is to be wrapped in a {@code try} block.
7474      * @param cleanup the handle that is invoked in the finally block.
7475      *
7476      * @return a method handle embodying the {@code try-finally} block composed of the two arguments.
7477      * @throws NullPointerException if any argument is null
7478      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code cleanup} does not accept
7479      *          the required leading arguments, or if the method handle types do
7480      *          not match in their return types and their
7481      *          corresponding trailing parameters
7482      *
7483      * @see MethodHandles#catchException(MethodHandle, Class, MethodHandle)
7484      * @since 9
7485      */
7486     public static MethodHandle tryFinally(MethodHandle target, MethodHandle cleanup) {
7487         List<Class<?>> targetParamTypes = target.type().parameterList();
7488         Class<?> rtype = target.type().returnType();
7489 
7490         tryFinallyChecks(target, cleanup);
7491 
7492         // Match parameter lists: if the cleanup has a shorter parameter list than the target, add ignored arguments.
7493         // The cleanup parameter list (minus the leading Throwable and result parameters) must be a sublist of the
7494         // target parameter list.
7495         cleanup = dropArgumentsToMatch(cleanup, (rtype == void.class ? 1 : 2), targetParamTypes, 0);
7496 
7497         // Ensure that the intrinsic type checks the instance thrown by the
7498         // target against the first parameter of cleanup
7499         cleanup = cleanup.asType(cleanup.type().changeParameterType(0, Throwable.class));
7500 
7501         // Use asFixedArity() to avoid unnecessary boxing of last argument for VarargsCollector case.
7502         return MethodHandleImpl.makeTryFinally(target.asFixedArity(), cleanup.asFixedArity(), rtype, targetParamTypes);
7503     }
7504 
7505     private static void tryFinallyChecks(MethodHandle target, MethodHandle cleanup) {
7506         Class<?> rtype = target.type().returnType();
7507         if (rtype != cleanup.type().returnType()) {
7508             throw misMatchedTypes("target and return types", cleanup.type().returnType(), rtype);
7509         }
7510         MethodType cleanupType = cleanup.type();
7511         if (!Throwable.class.isAssignableFrom(cleanupType.parameterType(0))) {
7512             throw misMatchedTypes("cleanup first argument and Throwable", cleanup.type(), Throwable.class);
7513         }
7514         if (rtype != void.class && cleanupType.parameterType(1) != rtype) {
7515             throw misMatchedTypes("cleanup second argument and target return type", cleanup.type(), rtype);
7516         }
7517         // The cleanup parameter list (minus the leading Throwable and result parameters) must be a sublist of the
7518         // target parameter list.
7519         int cleanupArgIndex = rtype == void.class ? 1 : 2;
7520         if (!cleanupType.effectivelyIdenticalParameters(cleanupArgIndex, target.type().parameterList())) {
7521             throw misMatchedTypes("cleanup parameters after (Throwable,result) and target parameter list prefix",
7522                     cleanup.type(), target.type());
7523         }
7524     }
